{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{bno055_8c_a86be0c8bef42d7ae350119844fe88e07} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{bno055_8h_a8eb62de24b0da2d87d0497c02f4ca797}{BNO055\+\_\+\+RETURN\+\_\+\+FUNCTION\+\_\+\+TYPE}} bno055\+\_\+get\+\_\+accel\+\_\+any\+\_\+motion\+\_\+durn (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{bno055_8h_aed742c436da53c1080638ce6ef7d13de}{u8}} \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{accel\+\_\+any\+\_\+motion\+\_\+durn\+\_\+u8}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This API used to read the accel anymotion duration from page one register from 0x12 bit 0 to 1. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em accel\+\_\+any\+\_\+motion\+\_\+durn\+\_\+u8} & \+: The value of accel anymotion duration {\begin{tabularx}{\linewidth}{|*{2}{>{\raggedright\arraybackslash}X|}}\hline
\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ accel\+\_\+any\+\_\+motion\+\_\+durn\+\_\+u8  }&\PBS\centering \cellcolor{\tableheadbgcolor}\textbf{ result  }\\\cline{1-2}
0x01  &BNO055\+\_\+\+BIT\+\_\+\+ENABLE  \\\cline{1-2}
0x00  &BNO055\+\_\+\+BIT\+\_\+\+DISABLE  \\\cline{1-2}
\end{tabularx}}
\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
results of bus communication function 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} BNO055\+\_\+\+SUCCESS \\
\hline
{\em 1} & -\/\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} BNO055\+\_\+\+ERROR \\
